<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_gbhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_gbhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_gbhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="default-checked" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#default-checked"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Default Checked</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">defaultChecked</code> prop to set the initial checked state in an uncontrolled manner. The checkbox will manage its
own state internally.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_ghhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_ghhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_ghhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">checked</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onCheckedChange</code> props to programatically control the checkbox&#x27;s state.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_gnhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_gnhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_gnhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the checkbox is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useCheckbox</code> hook. This way
you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_gthanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_gthanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_gthanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="disabled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#disabled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Disabled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">disabled</code> prop to make the checkbox non-interactive.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_h3hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_h3hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_h3hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="indeterminate" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#indeterminate"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Indeterminate</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">indeterminate</code> prop to create a checkbox in an indeterminate state (partially checked).</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_h9hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_h9hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_h9hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="field" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#field"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Field</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The checkbox integrates smoothly with the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Field</code> component to handle form state, helper text, and error text for proper
accessibility.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_hfhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_hfhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_hfhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="form" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#form"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Form</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Pass the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">name</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">value</code> props to the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Checkbox.Root</code> component to make the checkbox part of a form. The checkbox&#x27;s
value will be submitted with the form when the user submits it.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_hlhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_hlhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_hlhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Access the checkbox&#x27;s state and methods with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Checkbox.Context</code> or the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useCheckboxContext</code> hook.</p>

<h2 id="checkbox-group" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#checkbox-group"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Checkbox Group</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Checkbox.Group</code> component to manage a group of checkboxes. The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Checkbox.Group</code> component manages the state of
the checkboxes and provides a way to access the checked values.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Checkbox.Group</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Checkbox.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Checkbox.Control</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Checkbox.Indicator</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Checkbox.Control</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Checkbox.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>

<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_i3hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_i3hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_i3hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled-1" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled-1"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">value</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChange</code> props to programmatically control the checkbox group&#x27;s state. This example
demonstrates how to manage selected checkboxes in an array and display the current selection.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_i9hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_i9hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_i9hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider-1" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider-1"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useCheckboxGroup</code> hook to create the checkbox group store and pass it to the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Checkbox.GroupProvider</code>
component. This provides maximum control over the group programmatically, similar to how <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> works for
individual checkboxes.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_ifhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_ifhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_ifhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="invalid" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#invalid"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Invalid</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">invalid</code> prop on <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Checkbox.Group</code> to mark the entire group as invalid for validation purposes. This applies the
invalid state to all checkboxes within the group.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_ilhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_ilhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_ilhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="max-selected" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#max-selected"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Max Selected</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">maxSelectedValues</code> prop to limit the number of checkboxes that can be selected at once. Once the maximum is
reached, remaining checkboxes become disabled.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_irhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_irhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_irhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="select-all" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#select-all"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Select All</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Implement a &quot;select all&quot; checkbox that controls all checkboxes within a group. The parent checkbox automatically shows
an indeterminate state when some (but not all) items are selected, and becomes fully checked when all items are
selected.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_j1hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_j1hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_j1hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="form-1" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#form-1"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Form</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Checkbox.Group</code> component within a form to handle multiple checkbox values with form submission. The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">name</code>
prop ensures all selected values are collected as an array when the form is submitted using <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">FormData.getAll()</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_j7hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_j7hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_j7hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="fieldset" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#fieldset"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Fieldset</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Fieldset</code> component with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Checkbox.Group</code> to provide semantic grouping with legend, helper text, and error text
support.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_jdhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_jdhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_jdhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="guides" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#guides"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Guides</h2>
<h3 id="aschild-behavior" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#aschild-behavior"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>asChild Behavior</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Checkbox.Root</code> element of the checkbox is a <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">label</code> element. This is because the checkbox is a form control and
should be associated with a label to provide context and meaning to the user. Otherwise, the HTML and accessibility
structure will be invalid.</p>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">If you need to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">asChild</code> property, make sure that the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">label</code> element is the direct child of the
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Checkbox.Root</code> component.</p>
</blockquote>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">Root</h3><p class="text c_fg.muted">Renders a <code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&lt;label&gt;</code> element.</p><div <h3 id="context-1" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context-1"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>

<h2 id="accessibility" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accessibility</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Complies with the <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/checkbox/" class="link">Checkbox WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-support" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#keyboard-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Keyboard Support</h3>

the initial checked state in an uncontrolled manner. The checkbox will manage its\nown state internally.\n\n**Example: default-checked**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/react/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nexport const DefaultChecked = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cCheckbox.Root className={styles.Root} defaultChecked\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Indicator className={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/solid/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from `onCheckedChange` props to programatically control the checkbox's state.\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/react/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [checked, setChecked] = useState\u003cCheckbox.CheckedState\u003e(true)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cCheckbox.Root className={styles.Root} checked={checked} onCheckedChange={(e) =\u003e setChecked(e.checked)}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Indicator className={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/solid/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [checked, setChecked] = createSignal\u003cCheckbox.CheckedState\u003e(true)\n  return (\n    \u003cCheckbox.Root class={styles.Root} checked={checked()} onCheckedChange={(e) =\u003e setChecked(e.checked)}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Checkbox, type CheckboxCheckedState } from '@ark-ui/vue/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nconst checked = ref\u003cCheckboxCheckedState\u003e(true)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" v-model:checked=\"checked\"\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n        \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/svelte/checkbox'\n  import { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\n  let checked = $state(false)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cCheckbox.Root class={styles.Root} bind:checked\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the checkbox is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useCheckbox` hook. This way\nyou can access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox, useCheckbox } from '@ark-ui/react/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const checkbox = useCheckbox()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"vstack\"\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={checkbox}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckbox.Indicator className={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n            \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.RootProvider\u003e\n\n      {checkbox.checked ? (\n        \u003cbutton type=\"button\" onClick={() =\u003e checkbox.setChecked(false)} className={button.Root}\u003e\n          Uncheck\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      ) : (\n        \u003cbutton type=\"button\" onClick={() =\u003e checkbox.setChecked(true)} className={button.Root}\u003e\n          Check\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox, useCheckbox } from '@ark-ui/solid/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const checkbox = useCheckbox()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={checkbox}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n            \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.RootProvider\u003e\n\n      {checkbox().checked ? (\n        \u003cbutton type=\"button\" onClick={() =\u003e checkbox().setChecked(false)} class={button.Root}\u003e\n          Uncheck\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      ) : (\n        \u003cbutton type=\"button\" onClick={() =\u003e checkbox().setChecked(true)} class={button.Root}\u003e\n          Check\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Checkbox, useCheckbox } from '@ark-ui/vue/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n\nconst checkbox = useCheckbox()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"checkbox\"\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.RootProvider\u003e\n\n    \u003cbutton v-if=\"checkbox.checked\" :class=\"button.Root\" type=\"button\" @click=\"() =\u003e checkbox.setChecked(false)\"\u003e\n      Uncheck\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cbutton v-else :class=\"button.Root\" type=\"button\" @click=\"() =\u003e checkbox.setChecked(true)\"\u003eCheck\u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Checkbox, useCheckbox } from '@ark-ui/svelte/checkbox'\n  import { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n\n  const checkbox = useCheckbox()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={checkbox}\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.RootProvider\u003e\n\n  {#if checkbox().checked}\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e checkbox().setChecked(false)}\u003eUncheck\u003c/button\u003e\n  {:else}\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e checkbox().setChecked(true)}\u003eCheck\u003c/button\u003e\n  {/if}\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Disabled\n\nUse the `disabled` prop to make the checkbox non-interactive.\n\n**Example: disabled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/react/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Disabled = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cCheckbox.Root className={styles.Root} disabled\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Indicator className={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/solid/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Disabled = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cCheckbox.Root class={styles.Root} disabled\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/vue/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" disabled\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n        \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/svelte/checkbox'\n  import { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cCheckbox.Root class={styles.Root} disabled\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Indeterminate\n\nUse the `indeterminate` prop to create a checkbox in an indeterminate state (partially checked).\n\n**Example: indeterminate**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/react/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon, MinusIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Indeterminate = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cCheckbox.Root className={styles.Root} checked=\"indeterminate\"\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Indicator className={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} indeterminate\u003e\n        \u003cMinusIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/solid/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon, MinusIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Indeterminate = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cCheckbox.Root class={styles.Root} checked=\"indeterminate\"\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Control 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" checked=\"indeterminate\"\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Control \u003cCheckbox.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\" indeterminate\u003e\n        \u003cMinusIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n####      \u003cMinusIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCheckbox\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Field\n\nThe checkbox integrates smoothly with the `Field` component to handle form state, helper text, and error text for proper\naccessibility.\n\n**Example: with-field**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/react/checkbox'\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/react/field'\nimport { CheckIcon, MinusIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cField.Root className={field.Root} data-inline\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Indicator className={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} indeterminate\u003e\n          \u003cMinusIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText className={field.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText className={field.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/solid/checkbox'\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/solid/field'\nimport { CheckIcon, MinusIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cField.Root class={field.Root} data-inline\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} indeterminate\u003e\n          \u003cMinusIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText class={field.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText class={field.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/vue/checkbox'\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/vue/field'\nimport { CheckIcon, MinusIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cField.Root :class=\"field.Root\" data-inline\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\" indeterminate\u003e\n          \u003cMinusIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText :class=\"field.HelperText\"\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText :class=\"field.ErrorText\"\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/svelte/checkbox'\n  import { Field } from class={styles.Indicator} indeterminate\u003e\n        \u003cMinusIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n  \u003cField.HelperText class={field.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n  \u003cField.ErrorText class={field.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n\u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Form\n\nPass the `name` and `value` props to the `Checkbox.Root` component to make the checkbox part of a form. The checkbox's\nvalue will be submitted with the form when the user submits it.\n\n**Example: with-form**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/react/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n\nexport const WithForm = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cform\n    style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: '1rem', alignItems: 'flex-start' }}\n    onSubmit={(e) =\u003e {\n      e.preventDefault()\n      const formData = new FormData(e.currentTarget)\n      console.log('terms:', formData.get('terms'))\n    }}\n  \u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Root className={styles.Root} name=\"terms\" value=\"accepted\"\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Indicator className={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eI agree to the terms and conditions\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n    \u003cbutton className={button.Root} data-variant=\"solid\" type=\"submit\"\u003e\n      Submit\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/form\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/solid/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n\nexport const WithForm = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cform\n    style={{ display: 'flex', 'flex-direction': 'column', gap: '1rem', 'align-items': 'flex-start' }}\n    onSubmit={(e) =\u003e {\n      e.preventDefault()\n      const formData = new FormData(e.currentTarget)\n      console.log('terms:', formData.get('terms'))\n    }}\n  \u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Root class={styles.Root} name=\"terms\" value=\"accepted\"\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eI agree to the terms and conditions\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n    \u003cbutton class={button.Root} data-variant=\"solid\" type=\"submit\"\u003e\n      Submit\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/form\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/vue/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n\nconst handleSubmit = (event: Event) =\u003e {\n  event.preventDefault()\n  const formData = new FormData(event.target as HTMLFormElement)\n  console.log('terms:', formData.get('terms'))\n}\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cform style=\"display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 1rem; align-items: flex-start\" @submit=\"handleSubmit\"\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" name=\"terms\" value=\"accepted\"\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eI agree to the terms and conditions\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n    \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" data-variant=\"solid\" type=\"submit\"\u003eSubmit\u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/form\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/svelte/checkbox'\n  import { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cform\n  style=\"display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 1rem; align-items: flex-start;\"\n  onsubmit={(e) =\u003e {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    const formData = new FormData(e.currentTarget)\n    console.log('terms:', formData.get('terms'))\n  }}\n\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.Root class={styles.Root} name=\"terms\" value=\"accepted\"\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eI agree to the terms and conditions\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n  \u003cbutton class={button.Root} data-variant=\"solid\" type=\"submit\"\u003eSubmit\u003c/button\u003e\n\u003c/form\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Context\n\nAccess the checkbox's state and methods with `Checkbox.Context` or the `useCheckboxContext` hook.\n\n**Example: context**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/react/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cCheckbox.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Indicator className={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Context\u003e\n      {(checkbox) =\u003e \u003cCheckbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eChecked: {String(checkbox.checked)}\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e}\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Context\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/solid/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cCheckbox.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Context\u003e\n      {(checkbox) =\u003e \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eChecked: {String(checkbox().checked)}\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e}\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Context\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/vue/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n        \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Context v-slot=\"checkbox\"\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eChecked: {{ String(checkbox.checked) }}\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Context\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/svelte/checkbox'\n  import { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cCheckbox.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.Context\u003e\n    {#snippet render(api)}\n      \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eChecked: {String(api().checked)}\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n    {/snippet}\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Context\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n## Checkbox Group\n\nUse the `Checkbox.Group` component to manage a group of checkboxes. The `Checkbox.Group` component manages the state of\nthe checkboxes and provides a way to access the checked values.\n\n```tsx\n\u003cCheckbox.Group\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.Root\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Indicator /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Label /\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n\u003c/Checkbox.Group\u003e\n```\n\n**Example: group**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/react/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Group = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cCheckbox.Group className={styles.Group} defaultValue={['react']} name=\"framework\"\u003e\n    {items.map((item) =\u003e (\n      \u003cCheckbox.Root className={styles.Root} value={item.value} key={item.value}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckbox.Indicator className={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n            \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n    ))}\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Group\u003e\n)\n\nconst items = [\n  { label: 'React', value: 'react' },\n  { label: 'Solid', value: 'solid' },\n  { label: 'Vue', value: 'vue' },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/solid/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Group = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cCheckbox.Group class={styles.Group} defaultValue={['react']} name=\"framework\"\u003e\n    \u003cFor each={items}\u003e\n      {(item) =\u003e (\n        \u003cCheckbox.Root class={styles.Root} value={item.value}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n            \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n              \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n          \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n          \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n          \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/For\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Group\u003e\n)\n\nconst items = [\n  { label: 'React', value: 'react' },\n  { label: 'Solid', value: 'solid' },\n  { label: 'Vue', value: 'vue' },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/vue/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  { label: 'React', value: 'react' },\n  { label: 'Solid', value: 'solid' },\n  { label: 'Vue', value: 'vue' },\n]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.Group :class=\"styles.Group\" :defaultValue=\"['react']\" name=\"framework\"\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" v-for=\"item in items\" :value=\"item.value\" :key=\"item.value\"\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003e{{ item.label }}\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Group\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/svelte/checkbox'\n  import { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\n  const items = [\n    { label: 'React', value: 'react' },\n    { label: 'Solid', value: 'solid' },\n    { label: 'Vue', value: 'vue' },\n  ]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cCheckbox.Group class={styles.Group} defaultValue={['react']} name=\"framework\"\u003e\n  {#each items as item (item.value)}\n    \u003cCheckbox.Root class={styles.Root} value={item.value}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n  {/each}\n\u003c/Checkbox.Group\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controlled\n\nUse the `value` and `onValueChange` props to programmatically control the checkbox group's state. This example\ndemonstrates how to manage selected checkboxes in an array and display the current selection.\n\n**Example: group-controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/react/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nexport const GroupControlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [value, setValue] = useState(['react'])\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"vstack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003evalue: {JSON.stringify(value)}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Group className={styles.Group} value={value} name=\"framework\" onValueChange={setValue}\u003e\n        {items.map((item) =\u003e (\n          \u003cCheckbox.Root className={styles.Root} value={item.value} key={item.value}\u003e\n            \u003cCheckbox.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n              \u003cCheckbox.Indicator className={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n                \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n            \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n            \u003cCheckbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n            \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n          \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Group\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  { label: 'React', value: 'react' },\n  { label: 'Solid', value: 'solid' },\n  { label: 'Vue', value: 'vue' },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/solid/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { createSignal, For } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nexport const GroupControlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [value, setValue] = createSignal(['react'])\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003evalue: {JSON.stringify(value())}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Group class={styles.Group} value={value} onValueChange={setValue} name=\"framework\"\u003e\n        \u003cFor each={items}\u003e\n          {(item) =\u003e (\n            \u003cCheckbox.Root class={styles.Root} value={item.value}\u003e\n              \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n                \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n                  \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n                \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n              \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n              \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n              \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n            \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/For\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Group\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  { label: 'React', value: 'react' },\n  { label: 'Solid', value: 'solid' },\n  { label: 'Vue', value: 'vue' },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/vue/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nconst value = ref(['react'])\n\nconst items = [\n  { label: 'React', value: 'react' },\n  { label: 'Solid', value: 'solid' },\n  { label: 'Vue', value: 'vue' },\n]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n    \u003coutput\u003evalue: {{ JSON.stringify(value) }}\u003c/output\u003e\n    \u003cCheckbox.Group :class=\"styles.Group\" v-model=\"value\" name=\"framework\"\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" v-for=\"item in items\" :value=\"item.value\" :key=\"item.value\"\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n          \u003cCheckbox.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n            \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003e{{ item.label }}\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.Group\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/svelte/checkbox'\n  import { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\n  const items = [\n    { label: 'React', value: 'react' },\n    { label: 'Solid', value: 'solid' },\n    { label: 'Vue', value: 'vue' },\n  ]\n\n  let value = $state(['react'])\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n  \u003coutput\u003evalue: {JSON.stringify(value)}\u003c/output\u003e\n  \u003cCheckbox.Group class={styles.Group} bind:value name=\"framework\"\u003e\n    {#each items as item (item.value)}\n      \u003cCheckbox.Root class={styles.Root} value={item.value}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n            \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/Checkbox.Group\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nUse the `useCheckboxGroup` hook to create the checkbox group store and pass it to the `Checkbox.GroupProvider`\ncomponent. This provides maximum control over the group programmatically, similar to how `RootProvider` works for\nindividual checkboxes.\n\n**Example: group-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox, useCheckboxGroup } from '@ark-ui/react/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nexport const GroupProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const group = useCheckboxGroup({\n    defaultValue: ['react'],\n    name: 'framework',\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cCheckbox.GroupProvider className={styles.Group} value={group}\u003e\n      {items.map((item) =\u003e (\n        \u003cCheckbox.Root className={styles.Root} value={item.value} key={item.value}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckbox.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n            \u003cCheckbox.Indicator className={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n              \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n          \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n          \u003cCheckbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n          \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n      ))}\n    \u003c/Checkbox.GroupProvider\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  { label: 'React', value: 'react' },\n  { label: 'Solid', value: 'solid' },\n  { label: 'Vue', value: 'vue' },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox, useCheckboxGroup } from '@ark-ui/solid/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nexport const GroupProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const group = useCheckboxGroup({\n    defaultValue: ['react'],\n    name: 'framework',\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cCheckbox.GroupProvider class={styles.Group} value={group}\u003e\n      \u003cFor each={items}\u003e\n        {(item) =\u003e (\n          \u003cCheckbox.Root class={styles.Root} value={item.value}\u003e\n            \u003cCheckbox.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n              \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n                \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n            \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n            \u003cCheckbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n            \u003cCheckbox.HiddenInput /\u003e\n          \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/For\u003e\n    \u003c/Checkbox.GroupProvider\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  { label: 'React', value: 'react' },\n  { label: 'Solid', value: 'solid' },\n  { label: 'Vue', value: 'vue' },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Checkbox, useCheckboxGroup } from '@ark-ui/vue/checkbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/checkbox.module.css'\n\nconst group = useCheckboxGroup({\n  defaultValue: ['react'],\n  name: 'framework',\n})\n\nconst items = [\n  { label: 'React', value: 'react' },\n  { label: 'Solid', value: 'solid' },\n  { label: 'Vue', value: 'vue'
